<Time>1519116101614</Time><response>None</response>< Text>
When I was little, my grandfather would bring bagels to the house. He always brought western bagels to us, so they have a fond place in my heart. Western is excellent for bagels and cream cheese, bagel sandwiches, and a few other things. I am not fond of most of the pastries and cookies that they sell, but they tend to sell out the case every day so perhaps they're just not my thing. I personally feel the Egg bagels are the best in LA, but I have coworkers who prefer Goldsteins, so again it's a preference thing. The Sepulveda location is open 24 hours - it makes a good stop on the way home after a night out.< /Text>

<user_id>100312878239412553479< /user_id>< Review>
My girlfriend and I were hungry for some birrieria so we looked around and saw there was a small hole in the wall restaurant by the name of Birrieria Sinaloa. All I can say is we will return to this place again and again.

Birrieria Sinaloa is a small restaurant that is located near Old Town Victorville Memorial Cemetery. It can be hard to miss if you are not actively looking for it. The parking can be hard to find since it is a small location. You can try to park in the small parking space located a further down the street if you are coming from Mojave Dr but other than that, you will probably have to find a parking near the street or in the neighborhood.

The restaurant is small shop. It has a few tables for four and if you have more than four then they will try to accommodate space for you. My girlfriend and I went on a Sunday afternoon and it wasn't packed when we got in but it did start to get busy as we waited for our food.

The food selection was small but the quality was great. My girlfriend and I ordered four plebe carne tacos and two consomes. Plebe tacos are a soft and crunchy-ish taco if you are wondering what it is. The wait for the food was probably 10 minutes. The plebe tacos were amazing. There was a right amount of meat with cheese and guacamole to satisfy any taste buds. Then if you dipped the tacos with the consome, everything in that moment would just feel right. The restaurant also have onions, cilantro, and spices as garnishes to the tacos. Overall, the food is a reason to return to this restaurant.

The services was also great. We were tended as soon as we walked in. Although, there were no tables when we got in, they quickly cleaned one off and we were seated. The wait for the food was also fast, like I said, it was around 10 minutes. They asked if everything was great and tended to us when we needed it.

The only thing that I could think that is bad about this restaurant is that they don't clean their tables unless there are people coming in. I'm not sure how long some of the tables are but it seems like it was not tended too unless they need to make space. However, that reason is not a reason to miss this restaurant.

In so, Birrieria Sinaloa is a small hole in the wall restaurant. Don't let the exterior of this location throw you off as you will be missing out a great quality of food. If you are just craving birrieria or just visiting Victorville, then I would absolutely recommend this place to try!<//Review>

< Review>
I've been trying to get my washing machine repaired since late April... it's now May 30th, and the machine is still not repaired. After DOZENS of phone calls to Sears Protection Agreements Dept., then to Sears Escalations, I am still awash in the miasma of a total circus of incompetence.

Speaking to Sears telephone representatives found me talking to them on a "A is for apple, B is for ball" level, they would still consistently read back to me what I had told them incorrectly.  If I said, "On the 21st I had an appointment..." they would reply with "Yes sir, the 22nd." Maddening in the extreme.  Finally, on two separate occasions I asked to speak to a manager as I wished to make a formal complaint and ended up on hold, whereupon - surprise! - both times I was disconnected and the call dropped.  One rep told me my machine had been repaired and my case closed. One person told me they couldn't look into my issue further until the repairman had been to the house and made his determinations; I told him the repairman had been to the house yesterday which he had trouble comprehending.

One appointment was not kept (I took a day off work for it) at all, one appointment where the repairman turned up and only looked at my dryer - after I'd taken great pains to make it clear to Sears that he was to service two machines; my washer and my dyer - he then refused to look at the washer as it wasn't on his work order, one appointment where the repairman made his diagnosis and left - whereupon in the following two days Sears never heard back from him with any notes regarding his diagnosis & recommendations... this put me back to square one . How many Sears (and/or 3rd party contractors) does it take to change light bulb? Answer: a lot.

Sears had been sending me repairmen from their 3rd party contractor. I tried to point out to Sears that, effectively, they were paying the contractor to ruin Sears' reputation and make their customers angry.

I ultimately managed some traction when I spoke to the Overflow Dept. and a gentleman saw the copious notes on my account and decided this needed bumping up to the level of District Manager. A Sears repairman came out, made his verdict, ordered some parts, and now I'm waiting for parts to arrive... at which point I'll have to make another appointment for someone to come out and install them.

Trust me, there's much much more to all this but you get the picture. The whole system is a joke. In the past, I've bought every appliance from Sears; oven, cooktop, fridges, dishwasher, washer, dryer, water heater, but no more. If an item goes down on me, I don't want to have to haggle and nag to have it repaired in a remotely reasonable time frame.

I really don't believe this spectacular display of incompetence is unique to me, it must be endemic. So, beware.<//Review>

I originally called to schedule service for my ice maker.  I called Sears and spoke with a woman. She asked me questions regarding the problem.  She scheduled an appt for a week and a half later. I was told the service person scheduled to come could not perform that service & to reschedule. I was upset.  Called Sears and was hung up on 4 times even after talking to a supervisor.  I have been with Sears since 1970 and did not feel I should have been treated that way.  Finally my last call I talked with Ethan & asked him not to hang up on me.  He assured he would not & transferred me to a tech of which I convinced them to order a new ice maker and schedule an appt at this time, instead of waiting for the tech to come out to diagnose the problem, order the part, wait for it to come to my home & then schedule an appt.  By that time, i would have been without my ice maker for about 6 wks.  No good Sears repair practice.  The new ice maker was ordered and I received it by UPS about 3 days later.  Still had to wait another for 1 1/2 wks to get a tech to come out. The tech came, took about 15 mins to replace and another 15 to be sure it cooled and worked well.. The tech was great and this is the kind of repair service I have gotten over the year.  It seems to me as big as Sears is and the number of people needing jobs, they would be able to keep enough repair person to not to have to wait so long for repairs.  They are very happy to take my money for the contracts and to purchase products and services.  Thank you for reading this and if you have had problems, it might be good to do what I have done to get them going in the right direction.I usually do not write about this stuff but in this case, enough was enough. I just want to see Sears stay around for a long time.</Text>

< Text>
I don't know why the heck I have not already written a review for Hair Drezzers?!  I have been getting my hair done by Tori for over 4 years.  I remember looking at the website way back then and wondering if I was hip enough to get my hair done there..?  I was a soccer mom after all, and had not gotten my hair worked on in YEARS.
My first visit was right as I was ending a crappy relationship and asked Tori to cut off my waist length hair.  CUT IT ALL OFF, was my request.  She talked to me for quite a while to make sure it is REALLY what I wanted to do, and after I convinced her that I was ready to let it go- CHOP.  It was gone. I loved it. I fell in love with her, and the shop :)
Since then I have not been the greatest client.  I should be in more often then I am, but each time I come in Tori works her magic without making me feel like I have let my crazy hair go for too long. lol!  (oh, and I must mention that I have a big head, and A LOT of hair!)   Most of the time I just tell her to do whatever she wants; I trust her.  I have had it lightened, darkened, redder, blonder, browner, short, not too short, straightened, curled... and I have always leave happy.
From the time you walk in and Xia greets you at the counter, to Norman offering you a beverage, through your entire visit, everyone is friendly, down-to-earth, and they all make you feel beautiful :)   The shop is modern, well decorated, has nice lighting, and comfortable...
(The only thing I wish is that they offered more affordable products.  While I do LOVE Bumble and Bumble, it is just a bit too pricey for my budget...)< /Text>

< Text>
So you would think with a name like Hair Drezzers on Fire, the place would be gay friendly right? If not completely gay?  LOL

No it is not.

I started to go there about a year ago when I moved to San Diego and was pleased with the haircuts from Sarah Vaughn.

Today, I was in a pinch and needed a haircut, I made an appointment online with JT Gordon who is one of the few stylists there that also cuts men's hair. I got a call about 2 hours before my appointment by the salon manager saying that Sarah had shared information about me to JT, and he did not feel comfortable cutting my hair. WTF ???

Was it the fact that I was a young gay doctor who thought he was cute? Is that a reason to refuse to cut someones hair?

The manager said she could book me sometime next week with Sarah, but honestly after being refused a "haircut" for being "gay" or who knows what else, I decided to never go back there and spread the word about the these people.

The other reason this place deserved 1 star is the haughty attitude with ikea design. They are in the middle or Normal Heights and had a place slapped together like a college dorm. If you are going to be paying $55 dollars for a haircut, at least make the place nice.

Am I bitter? Yes, have never been really felt discrimination in San Diego until I went there. Funny with a name like "Hair Dressers on Fire" you would think Normal Heights Pride was based out of there.</Text>

<Review>Sepi's offers a great spot for a sandwich and beer. The atmosphere is dark and cozy (in a good way), and the staff is friendly. The food was better than I expected, too. The Italian 2.0 is hearty with cold cuts and has a great flavor. I'm not sure exactly what makes it one version better than a normal Italian, but I'll allow it. Their bread, too, is really good -- light and airy and not too filling. Prices are average for the area but maybe slightly high for a sandwich. Still, I can't say I regret it. Would dine again!</Review>< Pics>

< review>
A deli/sports pub right next to UCLA campus that has a fun environment especially if you want to open a cold one with the boys. They have decent pitcher deals during their evening happy hour that is from 7-10 PM. They have some delicious sandwiches as well but they are all over priced. Although, I can understand because it's Westwood, but competing sub-sandwich deli's nearby offer pretty much the same thing and are a bit more inexpensive.</review>

< Text>
Sepi's is the heart and soul of UCLA and Westwood. There is no better place to watch a game or play a game with a group of friends. The staff (shoutout to Pancho) is very friendly, the beer is premier and the food is great as well. Highly recommend to all UCLA students as well as Westwood professionals. My favorite place over four years at UCLA, not to mention it's the oldest establishment in Westwood as well as the only place you can get a pitcher of beer in the village.</Text>
